GT: F0*sin(t) - beta*sin(x)*v - c0*beta*v - mu*(c1 - x**c2)*v - omega0**c3*x*exp(-Abs(x))
Candidate formulas: 50

GT (fixed) is:
\[
0.2647138982\,\sin t\;-\;0.3778288376\,v\sin x\;-\;0.7556576753\,v\;-\;0.7480073028\,v(1-x^2)\;-\;3.8704902421\,x e^{-|x|}
\]
Rewrite the \(v\)-polynomial part:
\[
-0.7480073028\,v(1-x^2) = -0.7480073028\,v + 0.7480073028\,v x^2
\]
So GT contains exactly these structural pieces:
- a pure \(\sin(t)\) term (no \(x\) dependence in its amplitude),
- a \(v\sin(x)\) term,
- a linear \(v\) term,
- a \(v x^2\) term,
- and a non-polynomial/non-rational damping term \(x e^{-|x|}\) (crucial).

Any candidate must be able to produce **both** \(v\sin(x)\) and \(x e^{-|x|}\) to be globally equivalent (domain includes negative \(x\), so \(|x|\) matters and cannot be dropped).

Now check candidates:

1. Polynomial in \(x,v\) + \(\sin(\text{affine }t)\). No \(v\sin(x)\). No \(x e^{-|x|}\). Cannot match.
2. Has \(v\), \(\sin(\text{affine }t)\), \(v^4\), \(x^{c6}\), \(v x^2\), \(x\). Still no \(v\sin(x)\), no \(x e^{-|x|}\). Cannot.
3. Similar to (2). No \(v\sin(x)\), no \(x e^{-|x|}\). Cannot.
4. Similar. Cannot.
5. Similar. Cannot.
6. Polynomial + \(\sin(\text{affine }t)\) + constant. No \(v\sin(x)\), no \(x e^{-|x|}\). Cannot.
7. Has rational \(x/(c8+x^2)\) and powers. Still no \(v\sin(x)\), no \(x e^{-|x|}\). Cannot.
8. Polynomial/power terms + \(\sin(\text{affine }t)\). No \(v\sin(x)\), no \(x e^{-|x|}\). Cannot.
9. Rational in \(x\) with \((c1+x^2)\) denominators, plus \(\sin(\cdot)\), plus \(v/(c9+|v|)\). No \(v\sin(x)\). No \(x e^{-|x|}\). Cannot.
10. Same issue. Cannot.
11. Rational + \(v^3,v\) + time-sines divided by \((c1+x^2)\). No \(v\sin(x)\). No \(x e^{-|x|}\). Cannot.
12. Same. Cannot.
13. Adds \(\log(c7 v+1)\). Still no \(v\sin(x)\), no \(x e^{-|x|}\). Cannot.
14. Same. Cannot.
15. Has \(v^{c4}\) and \(\sin(\text{affine }t)\). No \(v\sin(x)\), no \(x e^{-|x|}\). Cannot.

19. Polynomial with \(v x\) (not \(v\sin x\)) and \(x\) terms. No \(x e^{-|x|}\). Cannot.
20. Has \(x/(c5+x^2)\), \(v x^2\), \(x^{c9}\), \(\sin(\text{affine }t)\). No \(v\sin(x)\), no \(x e^{-|x|}\). Cannot.

50. Has \(v\), \(v x^2\), time-sines over \((c1+x^2)\), and \(v x^2/(c1+x^2)\). No \(v\sin(x)\), no \(x e^{-|x|}\). Cannot.

Trig phase shifts: many candidates have \(\sin(c2 t+c3)\) which can match \(0.2647\sin t\) by setting \(c2=1\), \(c3=0\) (or phase-shifted equivalents). But **none** of the candidates include \(\sin(x)\) multiplied by \(v\), and **none** include the essential \(x e^{-|x|}\) structure (exponential of \(|x|\)). Those missing functional forms cannot be created by tuning constants.

Conclusion: No match

GT Equivalence Verification (PO43)
============================================================
GT: F0*sin(t) - beta*sin(x)*v - c0*beta*v - mu*(c1 - x**c2)*v - omega0**c3*x*exp(-Abs(x))
Candidates evaluated: 50
Matched candidate IDs: []
Matched candidates: []

I need to analyze each candidate against the Ground Truth (GT):

**GT:** `-0.748007302808642*v*(1 - x**2) - 0.377828837635262*v*sin(x) - 0.755657675270524*v - 3.87049024210282*x*exp(-Abs(x)) + 0.26471389821047*sin(t)`

Let me expand this:
`0.748007302808642*v*x**2 - 0.748007302808642*v - 0.377828837635262*v*sin(x) - 0.755657675270524*v - 3.87049024210282*x*exp(-Abs(x)) + 0.26471389821047*sin(t)`

Combining v terms:
`0.748007302808642*v*x**2 - 1.503664978079166*v - 0.377828837635262*v*sin(x) - 3.87049024210282*x*exp(-Abs(x)) + 0.26471389821047*sin(t)`

The GT has these basis functions:
1. `v*x**2` - polynomial in v and x
2. `v` - linear in v
3. `v*sin(x)` - product of v and sin(x)
4. `x*exp(-Abs(x))` - product of x and exp(-|x|)
5. `sin(t)` - sinusoidal in t

Key observations:
- The term `v*sin(x)` is a unique basis function
- The term `x*exp(-Abs(x))` is a unique basis function
- No candidate can match unless it can represent both `v*sin(x)` and `x*exp(-Abs(x))`

Let me check if `x*exp(-Abs(x))` can be represented by `x/(c + x**2)`. These are different functions - `x*exp(-|x|)` decays exponentially while `x/(c+x²)` decays as 1/x. They are NOT equivalent.

Similarly, `v*sin(x)` cannot be represented by polynomial terms in v and x, or by `v*Abs(v)`, `v**3`, etc.

Let me now quickly scan all candidates:

**Candidates 1-8, 19-28, 35, 47-48:** These use polynomial/power-law terms in x and v (like `x**c`, `v**4`, `v**3`, `x**3`, `v*x**2`, `v*x`). None contain `v*sin(x)` or `x*exp(-Abs(x))`. They cannot match.

**Candidates 9-18, 20-21, 29-34, 36-46, 49-50:** These use `x/(c+x²)` type terms. The function `x/(c+x²)` is NOT equivalent to `x*exp(-|x|)` for any constant. Also, none contain `v*sin(x)`. They cannot match.

Let me verify more carefully for each candidate whether any combination of their terms could produce `v*sin(x)`:

None of the candidates contain `sin(x)` as a factor multiplied by `v`. The only `sin` functions present are `sin(t)` related terms. Since `sin(x)` and polynomial/rational functions of x are linearly independent, no combination of the available basis functions can produce `v*sin(x)`.

Therefore, **no candidate matches**.
